{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \mbox{\hyperlink{structt_e_m_a_c_d_m_a_descriptor}{t\+EMACDMADescriptor}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structt_e_m_a_c_d_m_a_descriptor}{t\+EMACDMADescriptor}}}



\doxysubsection{Function Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga8c6146307cd57b110ec319f0a6968bcf}\label{group__emac__api_ga8c6146307cd57b110ec319f0a6968bcf}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACAddrFilterGet@{EMACAddrFilterGet}}
\index{EMACAddrFilterGet@{EMACAddrFilterGet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACAddrFilterGet()}{EMACAddrFilterGet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t EMACAddr\+Filter\+Get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Index }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Gets filtering parameters associated with one of the configured MAC addresses.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Index} & is the index of the MAC address slot for which the filter is to be queried.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function returns filtering parameters associated with one of the MAC address slots that the controller supports. This configuration is used when perfect filtering (rather than hash table filtering) is selected.

Valid values for {\itshape ui32\+Index} are from 1 to (number of MAC address slots -\/ 1). The number of supported MAC address slots may be found by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga06aa7ee17a6c9cd21ab327167a74158e}{EMACNum\+Addr\+Get()}}. MAC index 0 is the local MAC address and does not have filtering parameters associated with it.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns the filter configuration as the logical OR of the following labels\+:
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+ADDR\+\_\+\+ENABLE}} indicates that this MAC address is enabled and is used when performing perfect filtering. If this flag is absent, the MAC address at the given index is disabled and is not used in filtering.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+SOURCE\+\_\+\+ADDR}} indicates that the MAC address at the given index is compared to the source address of incoming frames while performing perfect filtering. If absent, the MAC address is compared against the destination address.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+MASK\+\_\+\+BYTE\+\_\+6}} indicates that the MAC ignores the sixth byte of the source or destination address when filtering.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+MASK\+\_\+\+BYTE\+\_\+5}} indicates that the MAC ignores the fifth byte of the source or destination address when filtering.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+MASK\+\_\+\+BYTE\+\_\+4}} indicates that the MAC ignores the fourth byte of the source or destination address when filtering.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+MASK\+\_\+\+BYTE\+\_\+3}} indicates that the MAC ignores the third byte of the source or destination address when filtering.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+MASK\+\_\+\+BYTE\+\_\+2}} indicates that the MAC ignores the second byte of the source or destination address when filtering.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+MASK\+\_\+\+BYTE\+\_\+1}} indicates that the MAC ignores the first byte of the source or destination address when filtering. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga1d697d3dfb786cbbd2653c4f534d26f9}\label{group__emac__api_ga1d697d3dfb786cbbd2653c4f534d26f9}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACAddrFilterSet@{EMACAddrFilterSet}}
\index{EMACAddrFilterSet@{EMACAddrFilterSet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACAddrFilterSet()}{EMACAddrFilterSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACAddr\+Filter\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Index,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Config }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets filtering parameters associated with one of the configured MAC addresses.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Index} & is the index of the MAC address slot for which the filter is to be set. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Config} & sets the filter parameters for the given MAC address.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function sets filtering parameters associated with one of the MAC address slots that the controller supports. This configuration is used when perfect filtering (rather than hash table filtering) is selected.

Valid values for {\itshape ui32\+Index} are from 1 to (number of MAC address slots -\/ 1). The number of supported MAC address slots may be found by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga06aa7ee17a6c9cd21ab327167a74158e}{EMACNum\+Addr\+Get()}}. MAC index 0 is the local MAC address and does not have filtering parameters associated with it.

The {\itshape ui32\+Config} parameter determines how the given MAC address is used when filtering incoming Ethernet frames. It is comprised of a logical OR of the fields\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+ADDR\+\_\+\+ENABLE}} indicates that this MAC address is enabled and should be used when performing perfect filtering. If this flag is absent, the MAC address at the given index is disabled and is not used in filtering.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+SOURCE\+\_\+\+ADDR}} indicates that the MAC address at the given index is compared to the source address of incoming frames while performing perfect filtering. If absent, the MAC address is compared against the destination address.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+MASK\+\_\+\+BYTE\+\_\+6}} indicates that the MAC should ignore the sixth byte of the source or destination address when filtering.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+MASK\+\_\+\+BYTE\+\_\+5}} indicates that the MAC should ignore the fifth byte of the source or destination address when filtering.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+MASK\+\_\+\+BYTE\+\_\+4}} indicates that the MAC should ignore the fourth byte of the source or destination address when filtering.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+MASK\+\_\+\+BYTE\+\_\+3}} indicates that the MAC should ignore the third byte of the source or destination address when filtering.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+MASK\+\_\+\+BYTE\+\_\+2}} indicates that the MAC should ignore the second byte of the source or destination address when filtering.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+MASK\+\_\+\+BYTE\+\_\+1}} indicates that the MAC should ignore the first byte of the source or destination address when filtering.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gaf765810fcca3c99a4628b12f55ec50b3}\label{group__emac__api_gaf765810fcca3c99a4628b12f55ec50b3}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACAddrGet@{EMACAddrGet}}
\index{EMACAddrGet@{EMACAddrGet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACAddrGet()}{EMACAddrGet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACAddr\+Get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Index,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{pui8\+MACAddr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Gets one of the MAC addresses stored in the Ethernet controller.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Index} & is the zero-\/based index of the MAC address to return. \\
\hline
{\em pui8\+MACAddr} & is the pointer to the location in which to store the array of MAC-\/48 address octets.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function reads the currently programmed MAC address into the {\itshape pui8\+MACAddr} buffer. The {\itshape ui32\+Index} parameter defines which of the hardware\textquotesingle{}s MAC addresses to return. The number of MAC addresses supported by the controller may be queried using a call to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga06aa7ee17a6c9cd21ab327167a74158e}{EMACNum\+Addr\+Get()}}. Index 0 refers to the MAC address of the local node. Other indices are used to define MAC addresses when filtering incoming packets.

The address is written to the pui8\+MACAddr array ordered with the first byte to be transmitted in the first array entry. For example, if the address is written in its usual form with the Organizationally Unique Identifier (OUI) shown first as\+:

AC-\/\+DE-\/48-\/00-\/00-\/80

the data is returned with 0x\+AC in the first byte of the array, 0x\+DE in the second, 0x48 in the third and so on.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga40aad549556a636d8357446823da2f28}\label{group__emac__api_ga40aad549556a636d8357446823da2f28}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACAddrSet@{EMACAddrSet}}
\index{EMACAddrSet@{EMACAddrSet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACAddrSet()}{EMACAddrSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACAddr\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Index,  }\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{pui8\+MACAddr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the MAC address of the Ethernet controller.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the Ethernet controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Index} & is the zero-\/based index of the MAC address to set. \\
\hline
{\em pui8\+MACAddr} & is the pointer to the array of MAC-\/48 address octets.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function programs the IEEE-\/defined MAC-\/48 address specified in {\itshape pui8\+MACAddr} into the Ethernet controller. This address is used by the Ethernet controller for hardware-\/level filtering of incoming Ethernet packets (when promiscuous mode is not enabled). Index 0 is used to hold the local node\textquotesingle{}s MAC address which is inserted into all transmitted packets.

The controller may support several Ethernet MAC address slots, each of which may be programmed independently and used to filter incoming packets. The number of MAC addresses that the hardware supports may be queried using a call to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga06aa7ee17a6c9cd21ab327167a74158e}{EMACNum\+Addr\+Get()}}. The value of the {\itshape ui32\+Index} parameter must lie in the range from 0 to (number of MAC addresses -\/ 1) inclusive.

The MAC-\/48 address is defined as 6 octets, illustrated by the following example address. The numbers are shown in hexadecimal format. \begin{DoxyVerb}    AC-DE-48-00-00-80
\end{DoxyVerb}
 In this representation, the first three octets (AC-\/\+DE-\/48) are the Organizationally Unique Identifier (OUI). This is a number assigned by the IEEE to an organization that requests a block of MAC addresses. The last three octets (00-\/00-\/80) are a 24-\/bit number managed by the OUI owner to uniquely identify a piece of hardware within that organization that is to be connected to the Ethernet.

In this representation, the octets are transmitted from left to right, with the {\ttfamily AC\textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{} octet being transmitted first and the}80\textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{} octet being transmitted last. Within an octet, the bits are transmitted LSB to MSB. For this address, the first bit to be transmitted would be {\ttfamily 0\textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}, the LSB of}AC\textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}, and the last bit to be transmitted would be {\ttfamily 1\textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}, the MSB of }80\textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}.

The address passed to this function in the {\itshape pui8\+MACAddr} array is ordered with the first byte to be transmitted in the first array entry. For example, the address given above could be represented using the following array\+:

uint8\+\_\+t g\+\_\+pui8\+MACAddr\mbox{[}\mbox{]} = \{ 0x\+AC, 0x\+DE, 0x48, 0x00, 0x00, 0x80 \};

If the MAC address set by this function is currently enabled, it remains enabled following this call. Similarly, any filter configured for the MAC address remains unaffected by a change in the address.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga8ea1b279581199ef36b57397f5cf04b0}\label{group__emac__api_ga8ea1b279581199ef36b57397f5cf04b0}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACConfigGet@{EMACConfigGet}}
\index{EMACConfigGet@{EMACConfigGet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACConfigGet()}{EMACConfigGet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACConfig\+Get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{pui32\+Config,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{pui32\+Mode,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{pui32\+Rx\+Max\+Frame\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the Ethernet MAC\textquotesingle{}s current basic configuration parameters.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the Ethernet controller. \\
\hline
{\em pui32\+Config} & points to storage that is written with Ethernet MAC configuration. \\
\hline
{\em pui32\+Mode} & points to storage that is written with Ethernet MAC mode information. \\
\hline
{\em pui32\+Rx\+Max\+Frame\+Size} & points to storage that is written with the maximum receive frame size.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is called to query the basic operating parameters for the MAC and its DMA engines.

The {\itshape pui32\+Config} parameter is written with the logical OR of various fields and flags. The first field describes which MAC address is used during insertion or replacement for all transmitted frames. Valid options are


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+USE\+\_\+\+MACADDR1}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+USE\+\_\+\+MACADDR0}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

The interframe gap between transmitted frames is given using one of the following values\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+GAP\+\_\+96\+BITS}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+GAP\+\_\+88\+BITS}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+GAP\+\_\+80\+BITS}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+GAP\+\_\+72\+BITS}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+GAP\+\_\+64\+BITS}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+GAP\+\_\+56\+BITS}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+GAP\+\_\+48\+BITS}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+GAP\+\_\+40\+BITS}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

The number of bytes of preamble added to the beginning of every transmitted frame is described using one of the following values\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+7\+BYTE\+\_\+\+PREAMBLE}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+5\+BYTE\+\_\+\+PREAMBLE}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+3\+BYTE\+\_\+\+PREAMBLE}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

The back-\/off limit determines the range of the random time that the MAC delays after a collision and before attempting to retransmit a frame. One of the following values provides the currently selected limit. In each case the retransmission delay in terms of 512 bit time slots, is the lower of (2 $\ast$$\ast$ N) and a random number between 0 and the reported backoff-\/limit.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+BO\+\_\+\+LIMIT\+\_\+1024}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+BO\+\_\+\+LIMIT\+\_\+256}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+BO\+\_\+\+LIMIT\+\_\+16}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+BO\+\_\+\+LIMIT\+\_\+2}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

Handling of insertion or replacement of the source address in all transmitted frames is described by one of the following fields\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+SA\+\_\+\+INSERT}} causes the MAC address (0 or 1 depending on whether {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+USE\+\_\+\+MACADDR0}} or {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+USE\+\_\+\+MACADDR1}} was specified) to be inserted into all transmitted frames.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+SA\+\_\+\+REPLACE}} causes the MAC address to be replaced with the selected address in all transmitted frames.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+SA\+\_\+\+FROM\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTOR}} causes control of source address insertion or deletion to be controlled by fields in the DMA transmit descriptor, allowing control on a frame-\/by-\/frame basis.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Whether the interface attempts to operate in full-\/ or half-\/duplex mode is reported by one of the following flags\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+FULL\+\_\+\+DUPLEX}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+HALF\+\_\+\+DUPLEX}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

The following additional flags may also be included\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+2\+K\+\_\+\+PACKETS}} indicates that IEEE802.\+3as support for 2K packets is enabled. When present, the MAC considers all frames up to 2000 bytes in length as normal packets. When {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+JUMBO\+\_\+\+ENABLE}} is not reported, all frames larger than 2000 bytes are treated as Giant frames. The value of this flag should be ignored if {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+JUMBO\+\_\+\+ENABLE}} is also reported.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+STRIP\+\_\+\+CRC}} indicates that the 4-\/byte CRC of all Ethernet type frames is being stripped and dropped before the frame is forwarded to the application.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+JABBER\+\_\+\+DISABLE}} indicates that the the jabber timer on the transmitter is disabled, allowing frames of up to 16384 bytes to be transmitted. If this flag is absent, the MAC does not allow more than 2048 (or 10240 if {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+JUMBO\+\_\+\+ENABLE}} is reported) bytes to be sent in any one frame.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+JUMBO\+\_\+\+ENABLE}} indicates that Jumbo Frames of up to 9018 (or 9022 if using VLAN tagging) are enabled.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+CS\+\_\+\+DISABLE}} indicates that Carrier Sense is disabled during transmission when operating in half-\/duplex mode.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+100\+MBPS}} indicates that the MAC is using 100Mbps signaling to communicate with the PHY.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+OWN\+\_\+\+DISABLE}} indicates that reception of transmitted frames is disabled when operating in half-\/duplex mode.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+LOOPBACK}} indicates that internal loopback is enabled.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+CHECKSUM\+\_\+\+OFFLOAD}} indicates that IPv4 header checksum checking and IPv4 or IPv6 TCP, UPD or ICMP payload checksum checking is enabled. The results of the checksum calculations are reported via status fields in the DMA receive descriptors.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+RETRY\+\_\+\+DISABLE}} indicates that retransmission is disabled in cases where half-\/duplex mode is in use and a collision occurs. This condition causes the current frame to be ignored and a frame abort to be reported in the transmit frame status.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+AUTO\+\_\+\+CRC\+\_\+\+STRIPPING}} indicates that the last 4 bytes (frame check sequence) from all Ether type frames are being stripped before frames are forwarded to the application.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+DEFERRAL\+\_\+\+CHK\+\_\+\+ENABLE}} indicates that transmit deferral checking is disabled in half-\/duplex mode. When enabled, the transmitter reports an error if it is unable to transmit a frame for more than 24288 bit times (or 155680 bit times in Jumbo frame mode) due to an active carrier sense signal on the MII.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+ENABLED}} indicates that the MAC transmitter is currently enabled.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+ENABLED}} indicates that the MAC receiver is currently enabled.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The {\itshape pui32\+Mode\+Flags} parameter is written with operating parameters related to the internal MAC FIFOs. It comprises a logical OR of the following fields. The first field reports the transmit FIFO threshold. Transmission of a frame begins when this amount of data or a full frame exists in the transmit FIFO. This field should be ignored if {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+STORE\+\_\+\+FORWARD}} is also reported. One of the following values is reported\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+16\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+24\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+32\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+40\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+64\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+128\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+192\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+256\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

The second field reports the receive FIFO threshold. DMA transfers of received data begin either when the receive FIFO contains a full frame or this number of bytes. This field should be ignored if {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+STORE\+\_\+\+FORWARD}} is included. One of the following values is reported\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+64\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+32\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+96\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+128\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

The following additional flags may be included\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+KEEP\+\_\+\+BAD\+\_\+\+CRC}} indicates that frames with TCP/\+IP checksum errors are being forwarded to the application if those frames do not have any errors (including FCS errors) in the Ethernet framing. In these cases, the frames have errors only in the payload. If this flag is not reported, all frames with any detected error are discarded unless {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+FRAMES}} is also reported.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+STORE\+\_\+\+FORWARD}} indicates that the receive DMA is configured to read frames from the FIFO only after the complete frame has been written to it. If this mode is enabled, the receive threshold is ignored.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+FLUSH\+\_\+\+DISABLE}} indicates that the flushing of received frames is disabled in cases where receive descriptors or buffers are unavailable.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+STORE\+\_\+\+FORWARD}} indicates that the transmitter is configured to transmit a frame only after the whole frame has been written to the transmit FIFO. If this mode is enabled, the transmit threshold is ignored.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+FRAMES}} indicates that all frames other than runt error frames are being forwarded to the receive DMA regardless of any errors detected in the frames.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+UNDERSIZED\+\_\+\+FRAMES}} indicates that undersized frames (frames shorter than 64 bytes but with no errors) are being forwarded to the application. If this option is not reported, all undersized frames are dropped by the receiver unless it has already started transferring them to the receive FIFO due to the receive threshold setting.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+OPERATE\+\_\+2\+ND\+\_\+\+FRAME}} indicates that the transmit DMA is configured to operate on a second frame while waiting for the previous frame to be transmitted and associated status and timestamps to be reported. If absent, the transmit DMA works on a single frame at any one time, waiting for that frame to be transmitted and its status to be received before moving on to the next frame.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+ENABLED}} indicates that the transmit DMA engine is currently enabled.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+ENABLED}} indicates that the receive DMA engine is currently enabled.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The {\itshape pui32\+Rx\+Max\+Frame\+Size} is written with the currently configured maximum receive packet size. Packets larger than this are flagged as being in error.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gac5f841841defc3ca16794ca95508dcea}\label{group__emac__api_gac5f841841defc3ca16794ca95508dcea}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACConfigSet@{EMACConfigSet}}
\index{EMACConfigSet@{EMACConfigSet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACConfigSet()}{EMACConfigSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACConfig\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Config,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Mode\+Flags,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Rx\+Max\+Frame\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Configures basic Ethernet MAC operation parameters.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the Ethernet controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Config} & provides various flags and values configuring the MAC. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Mode\+Flags} & provides configuration relating to the transmit and receive DMA engines. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Rx\+Max\+Frame\+Size} & sets the maximum receive frame size above which an error is reported.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is called to configure basic operating parameters for the MAC and its DMA engines.

The {\itshape ui32\+Config} parameter is the logical OR of various fields and flags. The first field determines which MAC address is used during insertion or replacement for all transmitted frames. Valid options are


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+USE\+\_\+\+MACADDR1}} and
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+USE\+\_\+\+MACADDR0}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

The interframe gap between transmitted frames is controlled using one of the following values\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+GAP\+\_\+96\+BITS}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+GAP\+\_\+88\+BITS}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+GAP\+\_\+80\+BITS}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+GAP\+\_\+72\+BITS}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+GAP\+\_\+64\+BITS}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+GAP\+\_\+56\+BITS}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+GAP\+\_\+48\+BITS}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+GAP\+\_\+40\+BITS}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

The number of bytes of preamble added to the beginning of every transmitted frame is selected using one of the following values\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+7\+BYTE\+\_\+\+PREAMBLE}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+5\+BYTE\+\_\+\+PREAMBLE}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+3\+BYTE\+\_\+\+PREAMBLE}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

The back-\/off limit determines the range of the random time that the MAC delays after a collision and before attempting to retransmit a frame. One of the following values must be used to select this limit. In each case, the retransmission delay in terms of 512 bit time slots, is the lower of (2 $\ast$$\ast$ N) and a random number between 0 and the selected backoff-\/limit.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+BO\+\_\+\+LIMIT\+\_\+1024}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+BO\+\_\+\+LIMIT\+\_\+256}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+BO\+\_\+\+LIMIT\+\_\+16}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+BO\+\_\+\+LIMIT\+\_\+2}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

Control over insertion or replacement of the source address in all transmitted frames is provided by using one of the following fields\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+SA\+\_\+\+INSERT}} causes the MAC address (0 or 1 depending on whether {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+USE\+\_\+\+MACADDR0}} or {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+USE\+\_\+\+MACADDR1}} was specified) to be inserted into all transmitted frames.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+SA\+\_\+\+REPLACE}} causes the MAC address to be replaced with the selected address in all transmitted frames.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+SA\+\_\+\+FROM\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTOR}} causes control of source address insertion or deletion to be controlled by fields in the DMA transmit descriptor, allowing control on a frame-\/by-\/frame basis.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Whether the interface attempts to operate in full-\/ or half-\/duplex mode is controlled by one of the following flags\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+FULL\+\_\+\+DUPLEX}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+HALF\+\_\+\+DUPLEX}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

The following additional flags may also be specified\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+2\+K\+\_\+\+PACKETS}} enables IEEE802.\+3as support for 2K packets. When specified, the MAC considers all frames up to 2000 bytes in length as normal packets. When {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+JUMBO\+\_\+\+ENABLE}} is not specified, all frames larger than 2000 bytes are treated as Giant frames. This flag is ignored if {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+JUMBO\+\_\+\+ENABLE}} is specified.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+STRIP\+\_\+\+CRC}} causes the 4-\/byte CRC of all Ethernet type frames to be stripped and dropped before the frame is forwarded to the application.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+JABBER\+\_\+\+DISABLE}} disables the jabber timer on the transmitter and enables frames of up to 16384 bytes to be transmitted. If this flag is absent, the MAC does not allow more than 2048 (or 10240 if {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+JUMBO\+\_\+\+ENABLE}} is specified) bytes to be sent in any one frame.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+JUMBO\+\_\+\+ENABLE}} enables Jumbo Frames, allowing frames of up to 9018 (or 9022 if using VLAN tagging) to be handled without reporting giant frame errors.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+100\+MBPS}} forces the MAC to communicate with the PHY using 100Mbps signaling. If this option is not specified, the MAC uses 10Mbps signaling. This speed setting is important when using an external RMII PHY where the selected rate must match the PHY\textquotesingle{}s setting which may have been made as a result of auto-\/negotiation. When using the internal PHY or an external MII PHY, the signaling rate is controlled by the PHY-\/ provided transmit and receive clocks.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+CS\+\_\+\+DISABLE}} disables Carrier Sense during transmission when operating in half-\/duplex mode.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+OWN\+\_\+\+DISABLE}} disables reception of transmitted frames when operating in half-\/duplex mode.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+LOOPBACK}} enables internal loopback.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+CHECKSUM\+\_\+\+OFFLOAD}} enables IPv4 header checksum checking and IPv4 or IPv6 TCP, UPD or ICMP payload checksum checking. The results of the checksum calculations are reported via status fields in the DMA receive descriptors.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+RETRY\+\_\+\+DISABLE}} disables retransmission in cases where half-\/duplex mode is in use and a collision occurs. This condition causes the current frame to be ignored and a frame abort to be reported in the transmit frame status.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+AUTO\+\_\+\+CRC\+\_\+\+STRIPPING}} strips the last 4 bytes (frame check sequence) from all Ether type frames before forwarding the frames to the application.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+DEFERRAL\+\_\+\+CHK\+\_\+\+ENABLE}} enables transmit deferral checking in half-\/duplex mode. When enabled, the transmitter reports an error if it is unable to transmit a frame for more than 24288 bit times (or 155680 bit times in Jumbo frame mode) due to an active carrier sense signal on the MII.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The {\itshape ui32\+Mode\+Flags} parameter sets operating parameters related to the internal MAC FIFOs. It comprises a logical OR of the following fields. The first selects the transmit FIFO threshold. Transmission of a frame begins when this amount of data or a full frame exists in the transmit FIFO. This field is ignored if {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+STORE\+\_\+\+FORWARD}} is included. One of the following must be specified\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+16\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+24\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+32\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+40\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+64\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+128\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+192\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+256\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

The second field controls the receive FIFO threshold. DMA transfers of received data begin either when the receive FIFO contains a full frame or this number of bytes. This field is ignored if {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+STORE\+\_\+\+FORWARD}} is included. One of the following must be specified\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+64\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+32\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+96\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD\+\_\+128\+\_\+\+BYTES}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

The following additional flags may be specified\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+KEEP\+\_\+\+BAD\+\_\+\+CRC}} causes frames with TCP/\+IP checksum errors to be forwarded to the application if those frames do not have any errors (including FCS errors) in the Ethernet framing. In these cases, the frames have errors only in the payload. If this flag is not specified, all frames with any detected error are discarded unless {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+FRAMES}} is also specified.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+STORE\+\_\+\+FORWARD}} causes the receive DMA to read frames from the FIFO only after the complete frame has been written to it. If this mode is enabled, the receive threshold is ignored.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+FLUSH\+\_\+\+DISABLE}} disables the flushing of received frames in cases where receive descriptors or buffers are unavailable.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+STORE\+\_\+\+FORWARD}} causes the transmitter to start transmitting a frame only after the whole frame has been written to the transmit FIFO. If this mode is enabled, the transmit threshold is ignored.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+FRAMES}} causes all frames other than runt error frames to be forwarded to the receive DMA regardless of any errors detected in the frames.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+UNDERSIZED\+\_\+\+FRAMES}} causes undersized frames (frames shorter than 64 bytes but with no errors) to the application. If this option is not selected, all undersized frames are dropped by the receiver unless it has already started transferring them to the receive FIFO due to the receive threshold setting.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+OPERATE\+\_\+2\+ND\+\_\+\+FRAME}} enables the transmit DMA to operate on a second frame while waiting for the previous frame to be transmitted and associated status and timestamps to be reported. If absent, the transmit DMA works on a single frame at any one time, waiting for that frame to be transmitted and its status to be received before moving on to the next frame.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The {\itshape ui32\+Rx\+Max\+Frame\+Size} parameter may be used to override the default setting for the maximum number of bytes that can be received in a frame before that frame is flagged as being in error. If the parameter is set to 0, the default hardware settings are applied. If non-\/zero, any frame received which is longer than the {\itshape ui32\+Rx\+Max\+Frame\+Size}, regardless of whether the MAC is configured for normal or Jumbo frame operation, is flagged as an error.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gada95d93a0772edd5a0e439739b630cec}\label{group__emac__api_gada95d93a0772edd5a0e439739b630cec}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACDMAStateGet@{EMACDMAStateGet}}
\index{EMACDMAStateGet@{EMACDMAStateGet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACDMAStateGet()}{EMACDMAStateGet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t EMACDMAState\+Get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the current states of the Ethernet MAC transmit and receive DMA engines.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function may be used to query the current states of the transmit and receive DMA engines. The return value contains two fields, one providing the transmit state and the other the receive state. Macros {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga8cc268b84119a82cf53c9c4a152eb747}{EMAC\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+STATE()}}}} and {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gab0b006cb87773a211d7c0d440b850b4f}{EMAC\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+STATE()}}}} may be used to extract these fields from the returned value. Alternatively, masks {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+TXSTAT\+\_\+\+MASK}} and {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+RXSTAT\+\_\+\+MASK}} may be used directly to mask out the individual states from the returned value.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns the states of the transmit and receive DMA engines. These states are ORed together into a single word containing one of\+:
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+TXSTAT\+\_\+\+STOPPED}} indicating that the transmit engine is stopped.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+TXSTAT\+\_\+\+RUN\+\_\+\+FETCH\+\_\+\+DESC}} indicating that the transmit engine is fetching the next descriptor.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+TXSTAT\+\_\+\+RUN\+\_\+\+WAIT\+\_\+\+STATUS}} indicating that the transmit engine is waiting for status from the MAC.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+TXSTAT\+\_\+\+RUN\+\_\+\+READING}} indicating that the transmit engine is currently transferring data from memory to the MAC transmit FIFO.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+TXSTAT\+\_\+\+RUN\+\_\+\+CLOSE\+\_\+\+DESC}} indicating that the transmit engine is closing the descriptor after transmission of the buffer data.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+TXSTAT\+\_\+\+TS\+\_\+\+WRITE}} indicating that the transmit engine is currently writing timestamp information to the descriptor.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+TXSTAT\+\_\+\+SUSPENDED}} indicating that the transmit engine is suspended due to the next descriptor being unavailable (owned by the host) or a transmit buffer underflow.
\end{DoxyItemize}

and one of\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+RXSTAT\+\_\+\+STOPPED}} indicating that the receive engine is stopped.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+RXSTAT\+\_\+\+RUN\+\_\+\+FETCH\+\_\+\+DESC}} indicating that the receive engine is fetching the next descriptor.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+RXSTAT\+\_\+\+RUN\+\_\+\+WAIT\+\_\+\+PACKET}} indicating that the receive engine is waiting for the next packet.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+RXSTAT\+\_\+\+SUSPENDED}} indicating that the receive engine is suspended due to the next descriptor being unavailable.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+RXSTAT\+\_\+\+RUN\+\_\+\+CLOSE\+\_\+\+DESC}} indicating that the receive engine is closing the descriptor after receiving a buffer of data.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+RXSTAT\+\_\+\+TS\+\_\+\+WRITE}} indicating that the transmit engine is currently writing timestamp information to the descriptor.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+RXSTAT\+\_\+\+RUN\+\_\+\+RECEIVING}} indicating that the receive engine is currently transferring data from the MAC receive FIFO to memory.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Additionally, a DMA bus error may be signaled using {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+ERROR}}. If this flag is present, the source of the error is identified using one of the following values which may be extracted from the return value using {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+ERR\+\_\+\+MASK\+:}} 


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+ERR\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+WRITE}} indicates that an error occurred when writing received data to memory.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+ERR\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+READ}} indicates that an error occurred when reading data from memory for transmission.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+ERR\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+DESC\+\_\+\+WRITE}} indicates that an error occurred when writing to the receive descriptor.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+ERR\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+DESC\+\_\+\+WRITE}} indicates that an error occurred when writing to the transmit descriptor.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+ERR\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+DESC\+\_\+\+READ}} indicates that an error occurred when reading the receive descriptor.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+ERR\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+DESC\+\_\+\+READ}} indicates that an error occurred when reading the transmit descriptor. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga42fddd6374aadeecbb713f67feca1df0}\label{group__emac__api_ga42fddd6374aadeecbb713f67feca1df0}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACFrameFilterGet@{EMACFrameFilterGet}}
\index{EMACFrameFilterGet@{EMACFrameFilterGet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACFrameFilterGet()}{EMACFrameFilterGet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t EMACFrame\+Filter\+Get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the current Ethernet frame filtering settings.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function may be called to retrieve the frame filtering configuration set using a prior call to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gae3375d0773f4fd267119de1dcdc6e703}{EMACFrame\+Filter\+Set()}}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns a value comprising the logical OR of various flags indicating the frame filtering options in use. Possible flags are\+:
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+ALL}} indicates that the MAC to is configured to pass all received frames regardless of whether or not they pass any address filter that is configured. The receive status word in the relevant DMA descriptor is updated to indicate whether the configured filter passed or failed for the frame.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+VLAN}} indicates that the MAC is configured to drop any frames which do not pass the VLAN tag comparison.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+AND\+\_\+\+PERFECT}} indicates that the MAC is configured to pass frames if they match either the hash filter or the perfect filter. If this flag is absent, frames passing based on the result of a single filter, the perfect filter if {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+MULTICAST}} or {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+UNICAST}} are clear or the hash filter otherwise.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+SADDR}} indicates that the MAC is configured to drop received frames when the source address field in the frame does not match the values programmed into the enabled SA registers.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+INV\+\_\+\+SADDR}} enables inverse source address filtering. When this option is specified, frames for which the SA does not match the SA registers are marked as passing the source address filter.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+BROADCAST}} indicates that the MAC is configured to discard all incoming broadcast frames.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+PASS\+\_\+\+MULTICAST}} indicates that the MAC is configured to pass all incoming frames with multicast destinations addresses.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+INV\+\_\+\+DADDR}} indicates that the sense of the destination address filtering for both unicast and multicast frames is inverted.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+MULTICAST}} indicates that destination address filtering of received multicast frames is enabled using the hash table. If absent, perfect destination address filtering is used. If used in conjunction with {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+AND\+\_\+\+PERFECT}}, this flag indicates that the hash filter should be used for incoming multicast packets along with the perfect filter.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+UNICAST}} indicates that destination address filtering of received unicast frames is enabled using the hash table. If absent, perfect destination address filtering is used. If used in conjunction with {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+AND\+\_\+\+PERFECT}}, this flag indicates that the hash filter should be used for incoming unicast packets along with the perfect filter.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+PROMISCUOUS}} indicates that the MAC is configured to operate in promiscuous mode where all received frames are passed to the application and the SA and DA filter status bits of the descriptor receive status word are always cleared.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Control frame filtering configuration is indicated by one of the following values which may be extracted from the returned value using the mask {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+PASS\+\_\+\+MASK\+:}} 


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+PASS\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+CTRL}} prevents any control frame from reaching the application.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+PASS\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+PAUSE}} passes all control frames other than PAUSE even if they fail the configured address filter.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+PASS\+\_\+\+ALL\+\_\+\+CTRL}} passes all control frames, including PAUSE even if they fail the configured address filter.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+PASS\+\_\+\+ADDR\+\_\+\+CTRL}} passes all control frames only if they pass the configured address filter. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gae3375d0773f4fd267119de1dcdc6e703}\label{group__emac__api_gae3375d0773f4fd267119de1dcdc6e703}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACFrameFilterSet@{EMACFrameFilterSet}}
\index{EMACFrameFilterSet@{EMACFrameFilterSet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACFrameFilterSet()}{EMACFrameFilterSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACFrame\+Filter\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Filter\+Opts }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets options related to Ethernet frame filtering.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Filter\+Opts} & is a logical OR of flags defining the required MAC address filtering options.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function allows various filtering options to be defined and allows an application to control which frames are received based on various criteria related to the frame source and destination MAC addresses or VLAN tagging.

The {\itshape ui32\+Filter\+Opts} parameter is a logical OR of any of the following flags\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+ALL}} configures the MAC to pass all received frames regardless of whether or not they pass any address filter that is configured. The receive status word in the relevant DMA descriptor is updated to indicate whether the configured filter passed or failed for the frame.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+VLAN}} configures the MAC to drop any frames that do not pass the VLAN tag comparison.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+AND\+\_\+\+PERFECT}} configures the MAC to filter frames based on both any perfect filters set and the hash filter if enabled using {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+UNICAST}} or {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+MULTICAST}}. In this case, only if both filters fail is the packet rejected. If this option is absent, only one of the filter types is used, as controlled by {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+UNICAST}} and {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+MULTICAST}} for unicast and multicast frames respectively.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+SADDR}} configures the MAC to drop received frames when the source address field in the frame does not match the values programmed into the enabled SA registers.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+INV\+\_\+\+SADDR}} enables inverse source address filtering. When this option is specified, frames for which the SA does not match the SA registers are marked as passing the source address filter.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+BROADCAST}} configures the MAC to discard all incoming broadcast frames.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+PASS\+\_\+\+MULTICAST}} configures the MAC to pass all incoming frames with multicast destinations addresses.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+INV\+\_\+\+DADDR}} inverts the sense of the destination address filtering for both unicast and multicast frames.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+MULTICAST}} enables destination address filtering of received multicast frames using the hash table. If absent, perfect destination address filtering is used. If used in conjunction with {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+AND\+\_\+\+PERFECT}}, this flag indicates that the hash filter should be used for incoming multicast packets along with the perfect filter.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+UNICAST}} enables destination address filtering of received unicast frames using the hash table. If absent, perfect destination address filtering is used. If used in conjunction with {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+AND\+\_\+\+PERFECT}}, this flag indicates that the hash filter should be used for incoming unicast packets along with the perfect filter.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+PROMISCUOUS}} configures the MAC to operate in promiscuous mode where all received frames are passed to the application and the SA and DA filter status bits of the descriptor receive status word are always cleared.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Control frame filtering may be configured by ORing one of the following values into {\itshape ui32\+Filter\+Opts\+:} 


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+PASS\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+CTRL}} prevents any control frame from reaching the application.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+PASS\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+PAUSE}} passes all control frames other than PAUSE even if they fail the configured address filter.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+PASS\+\_\+\+ALL\+\_\+\+CTRL}} passes all control frames, including PAUSE even if they fail the configured address filter.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+PASS\+\_\+\+ADDR\+\_\+\+CTRL}} passes all control frames only if they pass the configured address filter.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gaaefd8278587fdb5bd194914536a5f755}\label{group__emac__api_gaaefd8278587fdb5bd194914536a5f755}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACHashFilterBitCalculate@{EMACHashFilterBitCalculate}}
\index{EMACHashFilterBitCalculate@{EMACHashFilterBitCalculate}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACHashFilterBitCalculate()}{EMACHashFilterBitCalculate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t EMACHash\+Filter\+Bit\+Calculate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{pui8\+MACAddr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the bit number to set in the MAC hash filter corresponding to a given MAC address.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em pui8\+MACAddr} & points to a buffer containing the 6-\/byte MAC address for which the hash filter bit is to be determined.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function may be used to determine which bit in the MAC address hash filter to set to describe a given 6-\/byte MAC address. The returned value is a 6-\/bit number where bit 5 indicates which of the two hash table words is affected and the bottom 5 bits indicate the bit number to set within that word. For example, if 0x22 (100010b) is returned, this indicates that bit 2 of word 1 ({\itshape ui32\+Hash\+Hi} as passed to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gae9962073274d2713495ac6faf44f8947}{EMACHash\+Filter\+Set()}}) must be set to describe the passed MAC address.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns the bit number to set in the MAC hash table to describe the passed MAC address. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gab44716c352dd002494d1577857c399ca}\label{group__emac__api_gab44716c352dd002494d1577857c399ca}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACHashFilterGet@{EMACHashFilterGet}}
\index{EMACHashFilterGet@{EMACHashFilterGet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACHashFilterGet()}{EMACHashFilterGet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACHash\+Filter\+Get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{pui32\+Hash\+Hi,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{pui32\+Hash\+Lo }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the current MAC address hash filter table.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em pui32\+Hash\+Hi} & points to storage to be written with the upper 32 bits of the current 64-\/bit hash filter table. \\
\hline
{\em pui32\+Hash\+Lo} & points to storage to be written with the lower 32 bits of the current 64-\/bit hash filter table.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function may be used to retrieve the current 64-\/bit hash filter table from the MAC prior to making changes and setting the new hash filter via a call to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gae9962073274d2713495ac6faf44f8947}{EMACHash\+Filter\+Set()}}.

Hash table filtering allows many different MAC addresses to be filtered simultaneously at the cost of some false-\/positive results in the form of packets passing the filter when their MAC address was not one of those required. A CRC of the packet source or destination MAC address is calculated and the bottom 6 bits are used as a bit index into the 64-\/bit hash filter table. If the bit in the hash table is set, the filter is considered to have passed. If the bit is clear, the filter fails and the packet is rejected (assuming normal rather than inverse filtering is configured).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gae9962073274d2713495ac6faf44f8947}\label{group__emac__api_gae9962073274d2713495ac6faf44f8947}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACHashFilterSet@{EMACHashFilterSet}}
\index{EMACHashFilterSet@{EMACHashFilterSet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACHashFilterSet()}{EMACHashFilterSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACHash\+Filter\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Hash\+Hi,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Hash\+Lo }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the MAC address hash filter table.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Hash\+Hi} & is the upper 32 bits of the current 64-\/bit hash filter table to set. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Hash\+Lo} & is the lower 32 bits of the current 64-\/bit hash filter table to set.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function may be used to set the current 64-\/bit hash filter table used by the MAC to filter incoming packets when hash filtering is enabled. Hash filtering is enabled by passing {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+UNICAST}} and/or {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+MULTICAST}} in the {\itshape ui32\+Filter\+Opts} parameter to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gae3375d0773f4fd267119de1dcdc6e703}{EMACFrame\+Filter\+Set()}}. The current hash filter may be retrieved by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gab44716c352dd002494d1577857c399ca}{EMACHash\+Filter\+Get()}}.

Hash table filtering allows many different MAC addresses to be filtered simultaneously at the cost of some false-\/positive results (in the form of packets passing the filter when their MAC address was not one of those required). A CRC of the packet source or destination MAC address is calculated and the bottom 6 bits are used as a bit index into the 64-\/bit hash filter table. If the bit in the hash table is set, the filter is considered to have passed. If the bit is clear, the filter fails and the packet is rejected (assuming normal rather than inverse filtering is configured).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga453520ef2871a0eaef9068288c5cf9a1}\label{group__emac__api_ga453520ef2871a0eaef9068288c5cf9a1}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACInit@{EMACInit}}
\index{EMACInit@{EMACInit}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACInit()}{EMACInit()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACInit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Sys\+Clk,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Bus\+Config,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Rx\+Burst,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Tx\+Burst,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Desc\+Skip\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Initializes the Ethernet MAC and sets bus-\/related DMA parameters.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the Ethernet controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Sys\+Clk} & is the current system clock frequency in Hertz. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Bus\+Config} & defines the bus operating mode for the Ethernet MAC DMA controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Rx\+Burst} & is the maximum receive burst size in words. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Tx\+Burst} & is the maximum transmit burst size in words. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Desc\+Skip\+Size} & is the number of 32-\/bit words to skip between two unchained DMA descriptors. Values in the range 0 to 31 are valid.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function sets bus-\/related parameters for the Ethernet MAC DMA engines. It must be called after \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga6f369bdbe2e8ea108ef1398242030198}{EMACPHYConfig\+Set()}} and called again after any subsequent call to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga6f369bdbe2e8ea108ef1398242030198}{EMACPHYConfig\+Set()}}.

The {\itshape ui32\+Bus\+Config} parameter is the logical OR of various fields. The first sets the DMA channel priority weight\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+PRIO\+\_\+\+WEIGHT\+\_\+1}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+PRIO\+\_\+\+WEIGHT\+\_\+2}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+PRIO\+\_\+\+WEIGHT\+\_\+3}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+DMA\+\_\+\+PRIO\+\_\+\+WEIGHT\+\_\+4}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

The second field sets the receive and transmit priorities used when arbitrating between the Rx and Tx DMA. The priorities are Rx\+:Tx unless {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+PRIORITY}} is also specified, in which case they become Tx\+:Rx. The priority provided here is ignored if {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+PRIORITY\+\_\+\+FIXED}} is specified.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+PRIORITY\+\_\+1\+\_\+1}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+PRIORITY\+\_\+2\+\_\+1}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+PRIORITY\+\_\+3\+\_\+1}} 
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+PRIORITY\+\_\+4\+\_\+1}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

The following additional flags may also be defined\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+PRIORITY}} indicates that the transmit DMA should be higher priority in all arbitration for the system-\/side bus. If this is not defined, the receive DMA has higher priority.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+ADDR\+\_\+\+ALIGNED}} works in tandem with {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+FIXED\+\_\+\+BURST}} to control address alignment of AHB bursts. When both flags are specified, all bursts are aligned to the start address least significant bits. If {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+FIXED\+\_\+\+BURST}} is not specified, the first burst is unaligned but subsequent bursts are aligned to the address.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+ALT\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTORS}} indicates that the DMA engine should use the alternate descriptor format as defined in type {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{structt_e_m_a_c_d_m_a_descriptor}{t\+EMACDMADescriptor}}}}. If absent, the basic descriptor type is used. Alternate descriptors are required if using IEEE 1588-\/2008 advanced timestamping, VLAN or TCP/\+UDP/\+ICMP CRC insertion features. Note that, for clarity, \mbox{\hyperlink{emac_8h}{emac.\+h}} does not contain type definitions for the basic descriptor type. Please see the part datasheet for information on basic descriptor structures.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+PRIORITY\+\_\+\+FIXED}} indicates that a fixed priority scheme should be employed when arbitrating between the transmit and receive DMA for system-\/side bus access. In this case, the receive channel always has priority unless {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+PRIORITY}} is set, in which case the transmit channel has priority. If {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+PRIORITY\+\_\+\+FIXED}} is not specified, a weighted round-\/robin arbitration scheme is used with the weighting defined using {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+PRIORITY\+\_\+1\+\_\+1}}, {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+PRIORITY\+\_\+2\+\_\+1}}, {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+PRIORITY\+\_\+3\+\_\+1}} or {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+PRIORITY\+\_\+4\+\_\+1}}, and {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+PRIORITY}}.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+FIXED\+\_\+\+BURST}} indicates that fixed burst transfers should be used.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+BCONFIG\+\_\+\+MIXED\+\_\+\+BURST}} indicates that the DMA engine should use mixed burst types depending on the length of data to be transferred across the system bus.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The {\itshape ui32\+Rx\+Burst} and {\itshape ui32\+Tx\+Burst} parameters indicate the maximum number of words that the relevant DMA should transfer in a single transaction. Valid values are 1, 2, 4, 8, 16 and 32. Any other value results in undefined behavior.

The {\itshape ui32\+Desc\+Skip\+Size} parameter is used when the descriptor lists are using ring mode (where descriptors are contiguous in memory with the last descriptor marked with the {\bfseries{END\+\_\+\+OF\+\_\+\+RING}} flag) rather than chained mode (where each descriptor includes a field that points to the next descriptor in the list). In ring mode, the hardware uses the {\itshape ui32\+Desc\+Skip\+Size} to skip past any application-\/defined fields after the end of the hardware-\/ defined descriptor fields. The parameter value indicates the number of 32-\/bit words to skip after the last field of the hardware-\/defined descriptor to get to the first field of the next descriptor. When using arrays of either the {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{structt_e_m_a_c_d_m_a_descriptor}{t\+EMACDMADescriptor}}}} or {\bfseries{t\+EMACAlt\+DMADescriptor}} types defined for this driver, {\itshape ui32\+Desc\+Skip\+Size} must be set to 1 to skip the {\itshape pv\+Next} pointer added to the end of each of these structures. ~\newline
 Applications may modify these structure definitions to include their own application-\/specific data and modify {\itshape ui32\+Desc\+Skip\+Size} appropriately if desired.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga98a90c7fc24bcfd366f2e776d6192085}\label{group__emac__api_ga98a90c7fc24bcfd366f2e776d6192085}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACIntClear@{EMACIntClear}}
\index{EMACIntClear@{EMACIntClear}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACIntClear()}{EMACIntClear()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACInt\+Clear (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Int\+Flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Clears individual Ethernet MAC interrupt sources.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the Ethernet MAC. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Int\+Flags} & is the bit mask of the interrupt sources to be cleared.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function disables the indicated Ethernet MAC interrupt sources.

The {\itshape ui32\+Int\+Flags} parameter is the logical OR of any of the following\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+PHY}} indicates that the PHY has signaled a change of state. Software must read and write the appropriate PHY registers to enable, disable and clear particular notifications.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+EARLY\+\_\+\+RECEIVE}} indicates that the DMA engine has filled the first data buffer of a packet.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+BUS\+\_\+\+ERROR}} indicates that a fatal bus error has occurred and that the DMA engine has been disabled.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+EARLY\+\_\+\+TRANSMIT}} indicates that a frame to be transmitted has been fully written from memory into the MAC transmit FIFO.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+WATCHDOG}} indicates that a frame with length greater than 2048 bytes (of 10240 bytes in Jumbo Frame mode) was received.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+STOPPED}} indicates that the receive process has entered the stopped state.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+BUFFER}} indicates that the host owns the next buffer in the DMA\textquotesingle{}s receive descriptor list and the DMA cannot, therefore, acquire a buffer. The receive process is suspended and can be resumed by changing the descriptor ownership and calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga473bdac3a4d64d1b975785811d5ca38d}{EMACRx\+DMAPoll\+Demand()}}.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+RECEIVE}} indicates that reception of a frame has completed and all requested status has been written to the appropriate DMA receive descriptor.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+UNDERFLOW}} indicates that the transmitter experienced an underflow during transmission. The transmit process is suspended.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+OVERFLOW}} indicates that an overflow was experienced during reception.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+JABBER}} indicates that the transmit jabber timer expired. This condition occurs when the frame size exceeds 2048 bytes (or 10240 bytes in Jumbo Frame mode) and causes the transmit process to abort and enter the Stopped state.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+BUFFER}} indicates that the host owns the next buffer in the DMA\textquotesingle{}s transmit descriptor list and that the DMA cannot, therefore, acquire a buffer. Transmission is suspended and can be resumed by changing the descriptor ownership and calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga3cafbfbc7de989bec229f26765094dd5}{EMACTx\+DMAPoll\+Demand()}}.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+STOPPED}} indicates that the transmit process has stopped.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TRANSMIT}} indicates that transmission of a frame has completed and that all requested status has been updated in the descriptor.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Summary interrupt bits {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+NORMAL\+\_\+\+INT}} and {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+ABNORMAL\+\_\+\+INT}} are cleared automatically by the driver if any of their constituent sources are cleared. Applications do not need to explicitly clear these bits.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga3cd70572561d8348b6fd4da688cd9f98}\label{group__emac__api_ga3cd70572561d8348b6fd4da688cd9f98}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACIntDisable@{EMACIntDisable}}
\index{EMACIntDisable@{EMACIntDisable}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACIntDisable()}{EMACIntDisable()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACInt\+Disable (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Int\+Flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Disables individual Ethernet MAC interrupt sources.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the Ethernet MAC. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Int\+Flags} & is the bit mask of the interrupt sources to be disabled.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function disables the indicated Ethernet MAC interrupt sources.

The {\itshape ui32\+Int\+Flags} parameter is the logical OR of any of the following\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+PHY}} indicates that the PHY has signaled a change of state. Software must read and write the appropriate PHY registers to enable and disable particular notifications.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+EARLY\+\_\+\+RECEIVE}} indicates that the DMA engine has filled the first data buffer of a packet.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+BUS\+\_\+\+ERROR}} indicates that a fatal bus error has occurred and that the DMA engine has been disabled.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+EARLY\+\_\+\+TRANSMIT}} indicates that a frame to be transmitted has been fully written from memory into the MAC transmit FIFO.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+WATCHDOG}} indicates that a frame with length greater than 2048 bytes (of 10240 bytes in Jumbo Frame mode) was received.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+STOPPED}} indicates that the receive process has entered the stopped state.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+BUFFER}} indicates that the host owns the next buffer in the DMA\textquotesingle{}s receive descriptor list and the DMA cannot, therefore, acquire a buffer. The receive process is suspended and can be resumed by changing the descriptor ownership and calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga473bdac3a4d64d1b975785811d5ca38d}{EMACRx\+DMAPoll\+Demand()}}.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+RECEIVE}} indicates that reception of a frame has completed and all requested status has been written to the appropriate DMA receive descriptor.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+UNDERFLOW}} indicates that the transmitter experienced an underflow during transmission. The transmit process is suspended.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+OVERFLOW}} indicates that an overflow was experienced during reception.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+JABBER}} indicates that the transmit jabber timer expired. This condition occurs when the frame size exceeds 2048 bytes (or 10240 bytes in Jumbo Frame mode) and causes the transmit process to abort and enter the Stopped state.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+BUFFER}} indicates that the host owns the next buffer in the DMA\textquotesingle{}s transmit descriptor list and that the DMA cannot, therefore, acquire a buffer. Transmission is suspended and can be resumed by changing the descriptor ownership and calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga3cafbfbc7de989bec229f26765094dd5}{EMACTx\+DMAPoll\+Demand()}}.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+STOPPED}} indicates that the transmit process has stopped.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TRANSMIT}} indicates that transmission of a frame has completed and that all requested status has been updated in the descriptor.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TIMESTAMP}} indicates that an interrupt from the timestamp module has occurred. This precise source of the interrupt can be determined by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga5e9b445e03590ddce6cd94141e1cb125}{EMACTimestamp\+Int\+Status()}}, which also clears this bit.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Summary interrupt bits {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+NORMAL\+\_\+\+INT}} and {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+ABNORMAL\+\_\+\+INT}} are disabled automatically by the driver if none of their constituent sources are enabled. Applications do not need to explicitly disable these bits.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Timestamp-\/related interrupts from the IEEE 1588 module must be disabled independently by using a call to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gabe48c7fd3199f749acabc2b83a012d35}{EMACTimestamp\+Target\+Int\+Disable()}}.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga00e291f3d7162936f3d0317a1546db51}\label{group__emac__api_ga00e291f3d7162936f3d0317a1546db51}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACIntEnable@{EMACIntEnable}}
\index{EMACIntEnable@{EMACIntEnable}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACIntEnable()}{EMACIntEnable()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACInt\+Enable (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Int\+Flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Enables individual Ethernet MAC interrupt sources.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the Ethernet MAC. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Int\+Flags} & is the bit mask of the interrupt sources to be enabled.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function enables the indicated Ethernet MAC interrupt sources. Only the sources that are enabled can be reflected to the processor interrupt; disabled sources have no effect on the processor.

The {\itshape ui32\+Int\+Flags} parameter is the logical OR of any of the following\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+PHY}} indicates that the PHY has signaled a change of state. Software must read and write the appropriate PHY registers to enable and disable particular notifications.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+EARLY\+\_\+\+RECEIVE}} indicates that the DMA engine has filled the first data buffer of a packet.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+BUS\+\_\+\+ERROR}} indicates that a fatal bus error has occurred and that the DMA engine has been disabled.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+EARLY\+\_\+\+TRANSMIT}} indicates that a frame to be transmitted has been fully written from memory into the MAC transmit FIFO.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+WATCHDOG}} indicates that a frame with length greater than 2048 bytes (of 10240 bytes in Jumbo Frame mode) was received.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+STOPPED}} indicates that the receive process has entered the stopped state.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+BUFFER}} indicates that the host owns the next buffer in the DMA\textquotesingle{}s receive descriptor list and the DMA cannot, therefore, acquire a buffer. The receive process is suspended and can be resumed by changing the descriptor ownership and calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga473bdac3a4d64d1b975785811d5ca38d}{EMACRx\+DMAPoll\+Demand()}}.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+RECEIVE}} indicates that reception of a frame has completed and all requested status has been written to the appropriate DMA receive descriptor.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+UNDERFLOW}} indicates that the transmitter experienced an underflow during transmission. The transmit process is suspended.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+OVERFLOW}} indicates that an overflow was experienced during reception.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+JABBER}} indicates that the transmit jabber timer expired. This condition occurs when the frame size exceeds 2048 bytes (or 10240 bytes in Jumbo Frame mode) and causes the transmit process to abort and enter the Stopped state.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+BUFFER}} indicates that the host owns the next buffer in the DMA\textquotesingle{}s transmit descriptor list and that the DMA cannot, therefore, acquire a buffer. Transmission is suspended and can be resumed by changing the descriptor ownership and calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga3cafbfbc7de989bec229f26765094dd5}{EMACTx\+DMAPoll\+Demand()}}.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+STOPPED}} indicates that the transmit process has stopped.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TRANSMIT}} indicates that transmission of a frame has completed and that all requested status has been updated in the descriptor.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Summary interrupt bits {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+NORMAL\+\_\+\+INT}} and {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+ABNORMAL\+\_\+\+INT}} are enabled automatically by the driver if any of their constituent sources are enabled. Applications do not need to explicitly enable these bits.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Timestamp-\/related interrupts from the IEEE 1588 module must be enabled independently by using a call to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaf5fba26bb9e913012e907dd80a494096}{EMACTimestamp\+Target\+Int\+Enable()}}.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gac81628900772eda30e2865a84e09cdf6}\label{group__emac__api_gac81628900772eda30e2865a84e09cdf6}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACIntRegister@{EMACIntRegister}}
\index{EMACIntRegister@{EMACIntRegister}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACIntRegister()}{EMACIntRegister()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACInt\+Register (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{void($\ast$)(void)}]{pfn\+Handler }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Registers an interrupt handler for an Ethernet interrupt.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em pfn\+Handler} & is a pointer to the function to be called when the enabled Ethernet interrupts occur.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function sets the handler to be called when the Ethernet interrupt occurs. This function enables the global interrupt in the interrupt controller; specific Ethernet interrupts must be enabled via \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga00e291f3d7162936f3d0317a1546db51}{EMACInt\+Enable()}}. It is the interrupt handler\textquotesingle{}s responsibility to clear the interrupt source.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{group__interrupt__api_ga0a32aafea7f4904d2a64ee18b45f96c9}{Int\+Register()}} for important information about registering interrupt handlers.
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
