\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga5e9b445e03590ddce6cd94141e1cb125}\label{group__emac__api_ga5e9b445e03590ddce6cd94141e1cb125}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACTimestampIntStatus@{EMACTimestampIntStatus}}
\index{EMACTimestampIntStatus@{EMACTimestampIntStatus}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACTimestampIntStatus()}{EMACTimestampIntStatus()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t EMACTimestamp\+Int\+Status (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Reads the status of the Ethernet system time interrupt.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
When an Ethernet interrupt occurs and {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TIMESTAMP}} is reported bu \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga500e332f5be1c1351a53c13383d311d6}{EMACInt\+Status()}}, this function must be called to read and clear the timer interrupt status.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The return value is the logical OR of the values {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+TS\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TS\+\_\+\+SEC\+\_\+\+OVERFLOW}} and {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+TS\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TARGET\+\_\+\+REACHED}}.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+TS\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TS\+\_\+\+SEC\+\_\+\+OVERFLOW}} indicates that the second counter in the hardware timer has rolled over.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+TS\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TARGET\+\_\+\+REACHED}} indicates that the system time incremented past the value set in an earlier call to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaa1152f2b3931cbd7099733b31be3de75}{EMACTimestamp\+Target\+Set()}}. When this occurs, a new target time may be set and the interrupt re-\/enabled using calls to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaa1152f2b3931cbd7099733b31be3de75}{EMACTimestamp\+Target\+Set()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaf5fba26bb9e913012e907dd80a494096}{EMACTimestamp\+Target\+Int\+Enable()}}. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga97dcc4e449a9c148b2128d6e25d81bc9}\label{group__emac__api_ga97dcc4e449a9c148b2128d6e25d81bc9}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACTimestampPPSCommand@{EMACTimestampPPSCommand}}
\index{EMACTimestampPPSCommand@{EMACTimestampPPSCommand}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACTimestampPPSCommand()}{EMACTimestampPPSCommand()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACTimestamp\+PPSCommand (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{ui8\+Cmd }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sends a command to control the PPS output from the Ethernet MAC.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui8\+Cmd} & identifies the command to be sent.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function may be used to send a command to the MAC PPS (Pulse Per Second) controller when it is operating in command mode. Command mode is selected by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gada1ddd9fe06cee8737805eca72b4a09e}{EMACTimestamp\+PPSCommand\+Mode\+Set()}}. Valid commands are as follow\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+\+COMMAND\+\_\+\+NONE}} indicates no command.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+\+COMMAND\+\_\+\+START\+\_\+\+SINGLE}} indicates that a single high pulse should be generated when the system time reaches the current target time.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+\+COMMAND\+\_\+\+START\+\_\+\+TRAIN}} indicates that a train of pulses should be started when the system time reaches the current target time.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+\+COMMAND\+\_\+\+CANCEL\+\_\+\+START}} cancels any pending start command if the system time has not yet reached the programmed target time.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+\+COMMAND\+\_\+\+STOP\+\_\+\+AT\+\_\+\+TIME}} indicates that the current pulse train should be stopped when the system time reaches the current target time.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+\+COMMAND\+\_\+\+STOP\+\_\+\+NOW}} indicates that the current pulse train should be stopped immediately.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+\+COMMAND\+\_\+\+CANCEL\+\_\+\+STOP}} cancels any pending stop command if the system time has not yet reached the programmed target time.
\end{DoxyItemize}

In all cases, the width of the pulses generated is governed by the {\itshape ui32\+Width} parameter passed to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaaa072b7f8a3d6888cc1114e5a99db5db}{EMACTimestamp\+PPSPeriod\+Set()}}. If a command starts a train of pulses, the period of the pulses is governed by the {\itshape ui32\+Period} parameter passed to the same function. Target times associated with PPS commands are set by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaa1152f2b3931cbd7099733b31be3de75}{EMACTimestamp\+Target\+Set()}}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gada1ddd9fe06cee8737805eca72b4a09e}\label{group__emac__api_gada1ddd9fe06cee8737805eca72b4a09e}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACTimestampPPSCommandModeSet@{EMACTimestampPPSCommandModeSet}}
\index{EMACTimestampPPSCommandModeSet@{EMACTimestampPPSCommandModeSet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACTimestampPPSCommandModeSet()}{EMACTimestampPPSCommandModeSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACTimestamp\+PPSCommand\+Mode\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Config }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Configures the Ethernet MAC PPS output in command mode. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Config} & determines how the system target time is used.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The simple mode of operation offered by the PPS (Pulse Per Second) engine may be too restrictive for some applications. The second mode, however, allows complex pulse trains to be generated using commands that tell the engine to send individual pulses or start and stop trains if pulses. In this mode, the pulse width and period may be set arbitrarily based on ticks of the clock used to update the system time. Commands are triggered at specific times using the target time last set using a call to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaa1152f2b3931cbd7099733b31be3de75}{EMACTimestamp\+Target\+Set()}}.

The {\itshape ui32\+Config} parameter may be used to control whether the target time is used to trigger commands only or can also generate an interrupt to the CPU. Valid values are\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+\+TARGET\+\_\+\+INT}} configures the target time to only raise an interrupt and not to trigger any pending PPS command.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+\+TARGET\+\_\+\+PPS}} configures the target time to trigger a pending PPS command but not raise an interrupt.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+\+TARGET\+\_\+\+BOTH}} configures the target time to trigger any pending PPS command and also raise an interrupt.
\end{DoxyItemize}

To use command mode, an application must call this function to enable the mode, then call\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaaa072b7f8a3d6888cc1114e5a99db5db}{EMACTimestamp\+PPSPeriod\+Set()}} to set the desired pulse width and period then
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaa1152f2b3931cbd7099733b31be3de75}{EMACTimestamp\+Target\+Set()}} to set the time at which the next command is executed, and finally
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga97dcc4e449a9c148b2128d6e25d81bc9}{EMACTimestamp\+PPSCommand()}} to send a command to cause the pulse or pulse train to be started at the required time.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gaaa072b7f8a3d6888cc1114e5a99db5db}\label{group__emac__api_gaaa072b7f8a3d6888cc1114e5a99db5db}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACTimestampPPSPeriodSet@{EMACTimestampPPSPeriodSet}}
\index{EMACTimestampPPSPeriodSet@{EMACTimestampPPSPeriodSet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACTimestampPPSPeriodSet()}{EMACTimestampPPSPeriodSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACTimestamp\+PPSPeriod\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Period,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Width }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the period and width of the pulses on the Ethernet MAC PPS output.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Period} & is the period of the PPS output expressed in terms of system time update ticks. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Width} & is the width of the high portion of the PPS output expressed in terms of system time update ticks.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function may be used to control the period and duty cycle of the signal output on the Ethernet MAC PPS pin when the PPS generator is operating in command mode and a command to send one or more pulses has been executed. Command mode is selected by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gada1ddd9fe06cee8737805eca72b4a09e}{EMACTimestamp\+PPSCommand\+Mode\+Set()}}.

In simple mode, the PPS output signal frequency is controlled by the {\itshape ui32\+Freq\+Config} parameter passed to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gab22754779ba3d28d6e45ab35346ef1f7}{EMACTimestamp\+PPSSimple\+Mode\+Set()}}.

The {\itshape ui32\+Period} and {\itshape ui32\+Width} parameters are expressed in terms of system time update ticks. When the system time is operating in coarse update mode, each tick is equivalent to the system clock. In fine update mode, a tick occurs every time the 32-\/bit system time accumulator overflows and this, in turn, is determined by the value passed to the function \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaf58bcf48127a67c0eda8eb96319e8690}{EMACTimestamp\+Addend\+Set()}}. Regardless of the tick source, each tick increments the actual system time, queried using \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaf0990d59e2cbde1a18ec08df5fb1c49d}{EMACTimestamp\+Sys\+Time\+Get()}} by the subsecond increment value passed in the {\itshape ui32\+Sub\+Second\+Inc} to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaa1145b330c9da2d665730a51739a27d2}{EMACTimestamp\+Config\+Set()}}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gab22754779ba3d28d6e45ab35346ef1f7}\label{group__emac__api_gab22754779ba3d28d6e45ab35346ef1f7}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACTimestampPPSSimpleModeSet@{EMACTimestampPPSSimpleModeSet}}
\index{EMACTimestampPPSSimpleModeSet@{EMACTimestampPPSSimpleModeSet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACTimestampPPSSimpleModeSet()}{EMACTimestampPPSSimpleModeSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACTimestamp\+PPSSimple\+Mode\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Freq\+Config }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Configures the Ethernet MAC PPS output in simple mode.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Freq\+Config} & determines the frequency of the output generated on the PPS pin.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function configures the Ethernet MAC PPS (Pulse Per Second) engine to operate in its simple mode which allows the generation of a few, fixed frequencies and pulse widths on the PPS pin. If more complex pulse train generation is required, the MAC also provides a command-\/based PPS control mode that can be selected by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gada1ddd9fe06cee8737805eca72b4a09e}{EMACTimestamp\+PPSCommand\+Mode\+Set()}}.

The {\itshape ui32\+Freq\+Config} parameter may take one of the following values\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+\+SINGLE\+\_\+\+PULSE}} generates a single high pulse on the PPS output once per second. The pulse width is the same as the system clock period.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+1\+HZ}} generates a 1Hz signal on the PPS output. This option is not available if the system time subsecond counter is currently configured to operate in binary rollover mode.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+2\+HZ}}, {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+4\+HZ}}, {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+8\+HZ}}, {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+16\+HZ}}, {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+32\+HZ}}, {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+64\+HZ}}, {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+128\+HZ}}, {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+256\+HZ}}, {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+512\+HZ}}, {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+1024\+HZ}}, {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+2048\+HZ}}, {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+4096\+HZ}}, {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+8192\+HZ}}, {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+16384\+HZ}} generate the requested frequency on the PPS output in both binary and digital rollover modes.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+32768\+HZ}} generates a 32KHz signal on the PPS output. This option is not available if the system time subsecond counter is currently configured to operate in digital rollover mode.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Except when {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+\+SINGLE\+\_\+\+PULSE}} is specified, the signal generated on PPS has a duty cycle of 50\% when binary rollover mode is used for the system time subsecond count. In digital mode, the output frequency averages the value requested and is resynchronized each second. For example, if {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+PPS\+\_\+4\+HZ}} is selected in digital rollover mode, the output generates three clocks with 50 percent duty cycle and 268 ms period followed by a fourth clock of 195 ms period, 134 ms low and 61 ms high.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gaf0990d59e2cbde1a18ec08df5fb1c49d}\label{group__emac__api_gaf0990d59e2cbde1a18ec08df5fb1c49d}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACTimestampSysTimeGet@{EMACTimestampSysTimeGet}}
\index{EMACTimestampSysTimeGet@{EMACTimestampSysTimeGet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACTimestampSysTimeGet()}{EMACTimestampSysTimeGet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACTimestamp\+Sys\+Time\+Get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{pui32\+Seconds,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{pui32\+Sub\+Seconds }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Gets the current system time.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em pui32\+Seconds} & points to storage for the current seconds value. \\
\hline
{\em pui32\+Sub\+Seconds} & points to storage for the current subseconds value.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function may be used to get the current system time.

The meaning of {\itshape ui32\+Sub\+Seconds} depends on the current system time configuration. If \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaa1145b330c9da2d665730a51739a27d2}{EMACTimestamp\+Config\+Set()}} was previously called with the {\itshape EMAC\+\_\+\+TS\+\_\+\+DIGITAL\+\_\+\+ROLLOVER} configuration option, each bit in the {\itshape ui32\+Sub\+Seconds} value represents 1 ns. If {\itshape EMAC\+\_\+\+TS\+\_\+\+BINARY\+\_\+\+ROLLOVER} was specified instead, a {\itshape ui32\+Sub\+Seconds} bit represents 0.\+46 ns.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga19741d3f097a47771f92253167423926}\label{group__emac__api_ga19741d3f097a47771f92253167423926}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACTimestampSysTimeSet@{EMACTimestampSysTimeSet}}
\index{EMACTimestampSysTimeSet@{EMACTimestampSysTimeSet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACTimestampSysTimeSet()}{EMACTimestampSysTimeSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACTimestamp\+Sys\+Time\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Seconds,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Sub\+Seconds }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the current system time.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Seconds} & is the seconds value of the new system clock setting. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Sub\+Seconds} & is the subseconds value of the new system clock setting.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function may be used to set the current system time. The system clock is set to the value passed in the {\itshape ui32\+Seconds} and {\itshape ui32\+Sub\+Seconds} parameters.

The meaning of {\itshape ui32\+Sub\+Seconds} depends on the current system time configuration. If \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaa1145b330c9da2d665730a51739a27d2}{EMACTimestamp\+Config\+Set()}} was previously called with the {\itshape EMAC\+\_\+\+TS\+\_\+\+DIGITAL\+\_\+\+ROLLOVER} configuration option, each bit in the {\itshape ui32\+Sub\+Seconds} value represents 1 ns. If {\itshape EMAC\+\_\+\+TS\+\_\+\+BINARY\+\_\+\+ROLLOVER} was specified instead, a {\itshape ui32\+Sub\+Seconds} bit represents 0.\+46 ns.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga1ab9a4c5f22d7a0be9552dd747cd2d75}\label{group__emac__api_ga1ab9a4c5f22d7a0be9552dd747cd2d75}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACTimestampSysTimeUpdate@{EMACTimestampSysTimeUpdate}}
\index{EMACTimestampSysTimeUpdate@{EMACTimestampSysTimeUpdate}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACTimestampSysTimeUpdate()}{EMACTimestampSysTimeUpdate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACTimestamp\+Sys\+Time\+Update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Seconds,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Sub\+Seconds,  }\item[{bool}]{b\+Inc }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adjusts the current system time upwards or downwards by a given amount.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Seconds} & is the seconds value of the time update to apply. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Sub\+Seconds} & is the subseconds value of the time update to apply. \\
\hline
{\em b\+Inc} & defines the direction of the update.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function may be used to adjust the current system time either upwards or downwards by a given amount. The size of the adjustment is given by the {\itshape ui32\+Seconds} and {\itshape ui32\+Sub\+Seconds} parameter and the direction by the {\itshape b\+Inc} parameter. When {\itshape b\+Inc} is {\itshape true}, the system time is advanced by the interval given. When it is {\itshape false}, the time is retarded by the interval.

The meaning of {\itshape ui32\+Sub\+Seconds} depends on the current system time configuration. If \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaa1145b330c9da2d665730a51739a27d2}{EMACTimestamp\+Config\+Set()}} was previously called with the {\itshape EMAC\+\_\+\+TS\+\_\+\+DIGITAL\+\_\+\+ROLLOVER} configuration option, each bit in the subsecond value represents 1 ns. If {\itshape EMAC\+\_\+\+TS\+\_\+\+BINARY\+\_\+\+ROLLOVER} was specified instead, a subsecond bit represents 0.\+46 ns.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gabe48c7fd3199f749acabc2b83a012d35}\label{group__emac__api_gabe48c7fd3199f749acabc2b83a012d35}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACTimestampTargetIntDisable@{EMACTimestampTargetIntDisable}}
\index{EMACTimestampTargetIntDisable@{EMACTimestampTargetIntDisable}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACTimestampTargetIntDisable()}{EMACTimestampTargetIntDisable()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACTimestamp\+Target\+Int\+Disable (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Disables the Ethernet system time interrupt.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function may be used to disable any pending Ethernet system time interrupt previously scheduled using calls to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaa1152f2b3931cbd7099733b31be3de75}{EMACTimestamp\+Target\+Set()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaf5fba26bb9e913012e907dd80a494096}{EMACTimestamp\+Target\+Int\+Enable()}}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gaf5fba26bb9e913012e907dd80a494096}\label{group__emac__api_gaf5fba26bb9e913012e907dd80a494096}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACTimestampTargetIntEnable@{EMACTimestampTargetIntEnable}}
\index{EMACTimestampTargetIntEnable@{EMACTimestampTargetIntEnable}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACTimestampTargetIntEnable()}{EMACTimestampTargetIntEnable()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACTimestamp\+Target\+Int\+Enable (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Enables the Ethernet system time interrupt.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function may be used after \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaa1152f2b3931cbd7099733b31be3de75}{EMACTimestamp\+Target\+Set()}} to schedule an interrupt at some future time. The time reference for the function is the IEEE 1588 time as returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaf0990d59e2cbde1a18ec08df5fb1c49d}{EMACTimestamp\+Sys\+Time\+Get()}}. To generate an interrupt when the system time exceeds a given value, call this function to set the desired time, then \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaf5fba26bb9e913012e907dd80a494096}{EMACTimestamp\+Target\+Int\+Enable()}} to enable the interrupt. When the system time increments past the target time, an Ethernet interrupt with status {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TIMESTAMP}} is generated.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gaa1152f2b3931cbd7099733b31be3de75}\label{group__emac__api_gaa1152f2b3931cbd7099733b31be3de75}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACTimestampTargetSet@{EMACTimestampTargetSet}}
\index{EMACTimestampTargetSet@{EMACTimestampTargetSet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACTimestampTargetSet()}{EMACTimestampTargetSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACTimestamp\+Target\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Seconds,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Sub\+Seconds }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the target system time at which the next Ethernet timer interrupt is generated.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Seconds} & is the second value of the desired target time. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Sub\+Seconds} & is the subseconds value of the desired target time.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function may be used to schedule an interrupt at some future time. The time reference for the function is the IEEE 1588 time as returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaf0990d59e2cbde1a18ec08df5fb1c49d}{EMACTimestamp\+Sys\+Time\+Get()}}. To generate an interrupt when the system time exceeds a given value, call this function to set the desired time, then \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaf5fba26bb9e913012e907dd80a494096}{EMACTimestamp\+Target\+Int\+Enable()}} to enable the interrupt. When the system time increments past the target time, an Ethernet interrupt with status {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+TIMESTAMP}} is generated.

The accuracy of the interrupt timing depends on the Ethernet timer update frequency and the subsecond increment value currently in use. The interrupt is generated on the first timer increment that causes the system time to be greater than or equal to the target time set.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga20e05ae702cd5a5c209b12f4584ae950}\label{group__emac__api_ga20e05ae702cd5a5c209b12f4584ae950}}

When terminating operations on the Ethernet interface, this function should be called. This function disables the transmitter.

\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACTxDMACurrentDescriptorGet@{EMACTxDMACurrentDescriptorGet}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structt_e_m_a_c_d_m_a_descriptor}{t\+EMACDMADescriptor}} $\ast$ EMACTx\+DMACurrent\+Descriptor\+Get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga865e20117c232f6a10accc9d9dd550dd}\label{group__emac__api_ga865e20117c232f6a10accc9d9dd550dd}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACTxDMADescriptorListGet@{EMACTxDMADescriptorListGet}}
\index{EMACTxDMADescriptorListGet@{EMACTxDMADescriptorListGet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACTxDMADescriptorListGet()}{EMACTxDMADescriptorListGet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structt_e_m_a_c_d_m_a_descriptor}{t\+EMACDMADescriptor}} $\ast$ EMACTx\+DMADescriptor\+List\+Get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a pointer to the start of the DMA transmit descriptor list.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function returns a pointer to the head of the Ethernet MAC\textquotesingle{}s transmit DMA descriptor list. This value corresponds to the pointer originally set using a call to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gafcafa29a185f206deb1911bc4e9c121e}{EMACTx\+DMADescriptor\+List\+Set()}}.

\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gafcafa29a185f206deb1911bc4e9c121e}\label{group__emac__api_gafcafa29a185f206deb1911bc4e9c121e}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACTxDMADescriptorListSet@{EMACTxDMADescriptorListSet}}
\index{EMACTxDMADescriptorListSet@{EMACTxDMADescriptorListSet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACTxDMADescriptorListSet()}{EMACTxDMADescriptorListSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACTx\+DMADescriptor\+List\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structt_e_m_a_c_d_m_a_descriptor}{t\+EMACDMADescriptor}} $\ast$}]{p\+Descriptor }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the DMA transmit descriptor list pointer.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Descriptor} & points to the first DMA descriptor in the list to be passed to the transmit DMA engine.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function sets the Ethernet MAC\textquotesingle{}s transmit DMA descriptor list pointer. The {\itshape p\+Descriptor} pointer must point to one or more descriptor structures.

When multiple descriptors are provided, they can be either chained or unchained. Chained descriptors are indicated by setting the {\bfseries{DES0\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+CTRL\+\_\+\+CHAINED}} or {\bfseries{DES1\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+CTRL\+\_\+\+CHAINED}} bit in the relevant word of the transmit or receive descriptor. If this bit is clear, unchained descriptors are assumed.

Chained descriptors use a link pointer in each descriptor to point to the next descriptor in the chain.

Unchained descriptors are assumed to be contiguous in memory with a consistent offset between the start of one descriptor and the next. If unchained descriptors are used, the {\itshape pv\+Link} field in the descriptor becomes available to store a second buffer pointer, allowing each descriptor to point to two buffers rather than one. In this case, the {\itshape ui32\+Desc\+Skip\+Size} parameter to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga453520ef2871a0eaef9068288c5cf9a1}{EMACInit()}} must previously have been set to the number of words between the end of one descriptor and the start of the next. This value must be 0 in cases where a packed array of {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{structt_e_m_a_c_d_m_a_descriptor}{t\+EMACDMADescriptor}}}} structures is used. If the application wishes to add new state fields to the end of the descriptor structure, the skip size should be set to accommodate the newly sized structure.

Applications are responsible for initializing all descriptor fields appropriately before passing the descriptor list to the hardware.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga3cafbfbc7de989bec229f26765094dd5}\label{group__emac__api_ga3cafbfbc7de989bec229f26765094dd5}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACTxDMAPollDemand@{EMACTxDMAPollDemand}}
\index{EMACTxDMAPollDemand@{EMACTxDMAPollDemand}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACTxDMAPollDemand()}{EMACTxDMAPollDemand()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACTx\+DMAPoll\+Demand (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Orders the MAC DMA controller to attempt to acquire the next transmit descriptor.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the Ethernet controller.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function must be called to restart the transmitter if it has been suspended due to the current transmit DMA descriptor being owned by the host. Once the application writes new values to the descriptor and marks it as being owned by the MAC DMA, this function causes the hardware to attempt to acquire the descriptor and start transmission of the new data.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function flushes any data currently held in the Ethernet transmit FIFO. Data that has already been passed to the MAC for transmission is transmitted, possibly resulting in a transmit underflow or runt frame transmission.

\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga863edfd09a55c78f52a3f4f3815939fb}\label{group__emac__api_ga863edfd09a55c78f52a3f4f3815939fb}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACVLANHashFilterBitCalculate@{EMACVLANHashFilterBitCalculate}}
\index{EMACVLANHashFilterBitCalculate@{EMACVLANHashFilterBitCalculate}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACVLANHashFilterBitCalculate()}{EMACVLANHashFilterBitCalculate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t EMACVLANHash\+Filter\+Bit\+Calculate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{ui16\+Tag }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the bit number to set in the VLAN hash filter corresponding to a given tag.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui16\+Tag} & is the VLAN tag for which the hash filter bit number is to be determined.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function may be used to determine which bit in the VLAN hash filter to set to describe a given 12-\/ or 16-\/bit VLAN tag. The returned value is a 4-\/bit value indicating the bit number to set within the 16-\/bit VLAN hash filter. For example, if 0x02 is returned, this indicates that bit 2 of the hash filter must be set to pass the supplied VLAN tag.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns the bit number to set in the VLAN hash filter to describe the passed tag. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga10688b212012eaf1a24fead506e6eb56}\label{group__emac__api_ga10688b212012eaf1a24fead506e6eb56}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACVLANHashFilterGet@{EMACVLANHashFilterGet}}
\index{EMACVLANHashFilterGet@{EMACVLANHashFilterGet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACVLANHashFilterGet()}{EMACVLANHashFilterGet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t EMACVLANHash\+Filter\+Get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the current value of the hash filter used to control reception of VLAN-\/tagged frames.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function allows the current VLAN tag hash filter value to be returned. Additional VLAN tags may be added to this filter by setting the appropriate bits, determined by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga863edfd09a55c78f52a3f4f3815939fb}{EMACVLANHash\+Filter\+Bit\+Calculate()}}, and then calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga938f432d971b5380ac1d45972c78b77c}{EMACVLANHash\+Filter\+Set()}} to set the new filter value.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns the current value of the VLAN hash filter. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga938f432d971b5380ac1d45972c78b77c}\label{group__emac__api_ga938f432d971b5380ac1d45972c78b77c}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACVLANHashFilterSet@{EMACVLANHashFilterSet}}
\index{EMACVLANHashFilterSet@{EMACVLANHashFilterSet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACVLANHashFilterSet()}{EMACVLANHashFilterSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACVLANHash\+Filter\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Hash }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the hash filter used to control reception of VLAN-\/tagged frames.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Hash} & is the hash filter value to set.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function allows the VLAG tag hash filter to be set. By using hash filtering, several different VLAN tags can be filtered very easily at the cost of some false positive results that must be removed by software.

The hash filter value passed in {\itshape ui32\+Hash} may be built up by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga863edfd09a55c78f52a3f4f3815939fb}{EMACVLANHash\+Filter\+Bit\+Calculate()}} for each VLAN tag that is to pass the filter and then set each of the bits for which the numbers are returned by that function. Care must be taken when clearing bits in the hash filter due to the fact that there is a many-\/to-\/one correspondence between VLAN tags and hash filter bits.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gaa7f104bad0ee98101e8088f1e6fc3af6}\label{group__emac__api_gaa7f104bad0ee98101e8088f1e6fc3af6}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACVLANRxConfigGet@{EMACVLANRxConfigGet}}
\index{EMACVLANRxConfigGet@{EMACVLANRxConfigGet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACVLANRxConfigGet()}{EMACVLANRxConfigGet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t EMACVLANRx\+Config\+Get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{pui16\+Tag }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the currently-\/set options related to reception of VLAN-\/tagged frames.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em pui16\+Tag} & points to storage which is written with the currently configured VLAN tag used for perfect filtering.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function returns information on how the receiver is currently handling IEEE 802.\+1Q VLAN-\/tagged frames.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga072e2967d87ec29d255e61f95ab4d8b0}{EMACVLANRx\+Config\+Set()}}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns flags defining how VLAN-\/tagged frames are handled. The value is a logical OR of the following flags\+:
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+ENABLE}} indicates that hash filtering is enabled for VLAN tags. If this flag is absent, perfect filtering using the tag returned in {\itshape $\ast$pui16\+Tag} is performed.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+SVLAN\+\_\+\+ENABLE}} indicates that the receiver recognizes S-\/\+VLAN (Type = 0x88\+A8) frames as valid VLAN-\/tagged frames. If absent, only frames with type 0x8100 are considered valid VLAN frames.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+INVERSE\+\_\+\+MATCH}} indicates that the receiver passes all VLAN frames for which the tags do not match the {\itshape $\ast$pui16\+Tag} value. If this flag is absent, only tagged frames matching {\itshape $\ast$pui16\+Tag} are passed.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+12\+BIT\+\_\+\+TAG}} indicates that the receiver is comparing only the bottom 12 bits of {\itshape $\ast$pui16\+Tag} when performing either perfect or hash filtering of VLAN frames. If this flag is absent, all 16 bits of the frame tag are examined when filtering. If this flag is set and {\itshape $\ast$pui16\+Tag} has all bottom 12 bits clear, the receiver passes all frames with types 0x8100 or 0x88\+A8 regardless of the tag values they contain. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga072e2967d87ec29d255e61f95ab4d8b0}\label{group__emac__api_ga072e2967d87ec29d255e61f95ab4d8b0}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACVLANRxConfigSet@{EMACVLANRxConfigSet}}
\index{EMACVLANRxConfigSet@{EMACVLANRxConfigSet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACVLANRxConfigSet()}{EMACVLANRxConfigSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACVLANRx\+Config\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{ui16\+Tag,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Config }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets options related to reception of VLAN-\/tagged frames.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui16\+Tag} & is the IEEE 802.\+1Q VLAN tag expected for incoming frames. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Config} & determines how the receiver handles VLAN-\/tagged frames.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function configures the receiver\textquotesingle{}s handling of IEEE 802.\+1Q VLAN tagged frames. Incoming tagged frames are filtered using either a perfect filter or a hash filter. When hash filtering is disabled, VLAN frames tagged with the value of {\itshape ui16\+Tag} pass the filter and all others are rejected. The tag comparison may involve all 16 bits or only the 12-\/bit VLAN ID portion of the tag.

The {\itshape ui32\+Config} parameter is a logical OR of the following values\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+HASH\+\_\+\+ENABLE}} enables hash filtering for VLAN tags. If this flag is absent, perfect filtering using the tag supplied in {\itshape ui16\+Tag} is performed. The hash filter may be set using \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga938f432d971b5380ac1d45972c78b77c}{EMACVLANHash\+Filter\+Set()}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga863edfd09a55c78f52a3f4f3815939fb}{EMACVLANHash\+Filter\+Bit\+Calculate()}} may be used to determine which bits to set in the filter for given VLAN tags.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+SVLAN\+\_\+\+ENABLE}} causes the receiver to recognize S-\/\+VLAN (Type = 0x88\+A8) frames as valid VLAN-\/tagged frames. If absent, only frames with type 0x8100 are considered valid VLAN frames.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+\+INVERSE\+\_\+\+MATCH}} causes the receiver to pass all VLAN frames for which the tags do not match the supplied {\itshape ui16\+Tag} value. If this flag is absent, only tagged frames matching {\itshape ui16\+Tag} are passed.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+RX\+\_\+12\+BIT\+\_\+\+TAG}} causes the receiver to compare only the bottom 12 bits of {\itshape ui16\+Tag} when performing either perfect or hash filtering of VLAN frames. If this flag is absent, all 16 bits of the frame tag are examined when filtering. If this flag is set and {\itshape ui16\+Tag} has all bottom 12 bits clear, the receiver passes all frames with types 0x8100 or 0x88\+A8 regardless of the tag values they contain.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
To ensure that VLAN frames that fail the tag filter are dropped by the MAC, \mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gae3375d0773f4fd267119de1dcdc6e703}{EMACFrame\+Filter\+Set()}} must be called with the {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+VLAN}} flag set in the {\itshape ui32\+Filter\+Opts} parameter. If this flag is not set, failing VLAN packets are received by the application, but bit 10 of RDES0 ({\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+FRMFILTER\+\_\+\+VLAN}}) is clear indicating that the packet did not match the current VLAG tag filter.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_gaa7f104bad0ee98101e8088f1e6fc3af6}{EMACVLANRx\+Config\+Get()}}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_gaaece59d6d129ea03ce46f7304b7841ef}\label{group__emac__api_gaaece59d6d129ea03ce46f7304b7841ef}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACVLANTxConfigGet@{EMACVLANTxConfigGet}}
\index{EMACVLANTxConfigGet@{EMACVLANTxConfigGet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACVLANTxConfigGet()}{EMACVLANTxConfigGet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t EMACVLANTx\+Config\+Get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{pui16\+Tag }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns currently-\/selected options related to transmission of VLAN-\/tagged frames.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em pui16\+Tag} & points to storage that is written with the VLAN tag currently being used for insertion or replacement.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function returns information on the current settings related to VLAN tagging of transmitted frames.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{group__emac__api_ga2b6dc1c136744b5e83b018f94f831f38}{EMACVLANTx\+Config\+Set()}}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns flags describing the current VLAN configuration relating to frame transmission. The return value is a logical OR of the following values\+:
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+SVLAN}} indicates that the S-\/\+VLAN type (0x88\+A8) is being used when inserting or replacing tags in transmitted frames. If this label is absent, C-\/\+VLAN type (0x8100) is being used.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+USE\+\_\+\+VLC}} indicates that the transmitter is processing VLAN frames according to the VLAN control (VLC) value returned here. If this tag is absent, VLAN handling is controlled by fields in the transmit descriptor.
\end{DoxyItemize}

If {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+USE\+\_\+\+VLC}} is returned, one of the following four labels is also included to define the transmit VLAN tag handling. Note that this value may be extracted from the return value using the mask {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+VLC\+\_\+\+MASK}}.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+VLC\+\_\+\+NONE}} indicates that the transmitter is not performing VLAN tag insertion, deletion or replacement.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+VLC\+\_\+\+DELETE}} indicates that the transmitter is removing VLAN tags from all transmitted frames which contain them.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+VLC\+\_\+\+INSERT}} indicates that the transmitter is inserting a VLAN type and tag into all outgoing frames regardless of whether or not they already contain a VLAN tag.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+VLC\+\_\+\+REPLACE}} indicates that the transmitter is replacing the VLAN tag in all transmitted frames of type 0x8100 or 0x88\+A8 with the value returned in {\itshape $\ast$pui16\+Tag}. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__emac__api_ga2b6dc1c136744b5e83b018f94f831f38}\label{group__emac__api_ga2b6dc1c136744b5e83b018f94f831f38}} 
\index{Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}!EMACVLANTxConfigSet@{EMACVLANTxConfigSet}}
\index{EMACVLANTxConfigSet@{EMACVLANTxConfigSet}!Emac\_api@{Emac\_api}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMACVLANTxConfigSet()}{EMACVLANTxConfigSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void EMACVLANTx\+Config\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Base,  }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{ui16\+Tag,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ui32\+Config }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets options related to transmission of VLAN-\/tagged frames.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ui32\+Base} & is the base address of the controller. \\
\hline
{\em ui16\+Tag} & is the VLAN tag to be used when inserting or replacing tags in transmitted frames. \\
\hline
{\em ui32\+Config} & determines the VLAN-\/related processing performed by the transmitter.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function is used to configure transmitter options relating to IEEE 802.\+1Q VLAN tagging. The transmitter may be set to insert tagging into untagged frames or replace existing tags with new values.

The {\itshape ui16\+Tag} parameter contains the VLAN tag to be used in outgoing tagged frames. The {\itshape ui32\+Config} parameter is a logical OR of the following labels\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+SVLAN}} uses the S-\/\+VLAN type (0x88\+A8) when inserting or replacing tags in transmitted frames. If this label is absent, C-\/\+VLAN type (0x8100) is used.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+USE\+\_\+\+VLC}} informs the transmitter that the VLAN tag handling should be defined by the VLAN control (VLC) value provided in this function call. If this tag is absent, VLAN handling is controlled by fields in the transmit descriptor.
\end{DoxyItemize}

If {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+USE\+\_\+\+VLC}} is set, one of the following four labels must also be included to define the transmit VLAN tag handling\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+VLC\+\_\+\+NONE}} instructs the transmitter to perform no VLAN tag insertion, deletion or replacement.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+VLC\+\_\+\+DELETE}} instructs the transmitter to remove VLAN tags from all transmitted frames that contain them. As a result, bytes 13, 14, 15 and 16 are removed from all frames with types 0x8100 or 0x88\+A8.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+VLC\+\_\+\+INSERT}} instructs the transmitter to insert a VLAN type and tag into all outgoing frames regardless of whether or not they already contain a VLAN tag.
\item {\bfseries{EMAC\+\_\+\+VLAN\+\_\+\+TX\+\_\+\+VLC\+\_\+\+REPLACE}} instructs the transmitter to replace the VLAN tag in all frames of type 0x8100 or 0x88\+A8 with the value provided to this function in the {\itshape ui16\+Tag} parameter.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None 
\end{DoxyReturn}
